## Issues & Possible Solutions

### 1. Flutter binding zone mismatch at startup

**Evidence**: 1 FlutterError event(s), first at `2026-04-29T09:49:21.903807Z`.

**Likely root cause**: `WidgetsFlutterBinding.ensureInitialized()` is called outside the `runZonedGuarded` zone that later runs `runApp`.

**Possible solution**: Move binding initialization and bootstrap work into the guarded zone, or initialize the zone before calling Flutter bindings.

### 2. Bloc event dispatched without a handler

**Evidence**: 17 FlutterError event(s), first at `2026-04-29T09:53:45.136688Z`.

**Likely root cause**: A `StateChanged` event is added to a Bloc that does not register `on<StateChanged>`.

**Possible solution**: Add the missing event handler or remove/replace the dispatch site so the Bloc contract is explicit.

### 3. Backend/API responses with non-success statuses

**Evidence**: GET https://lastmile.fainzy.tech/v1/statistics/subentities/7/top-customers/ -> 404 x4; GET https://lastmile.fainzy.tech/v1/statistics/subentities/7/ -> 404 x4

**Likely root cause**: Some dashboard/statistics or store endpoints return non-2xx/3xx responses for the active store/session data.

**Possible solution**: Handle these responses as visible degraded states and verify backend support for the active subentity id.

### 4. Socket lifecycle emitted with empty store id

**Evidence**: 14 socket event(s) reference `store_/`.

**Likely root cause**: Lifecycle stop/disconnect can run before a store id is available or after it has been cleared.

**Possible solution**: Skip WSS logging/stop calls when store id is empty, or preserve the last known store id until socket teardown completes.
